       <img alt="Dv Kulb / Fight Club (1999) | IMDb: 8.9" data-src="http://img-2.onedio.com/img/719/bound/2r0/542c1b723f79027e36f0626a.jpg" src="/images/trans.png" style="margin-bottom: -32px; width: 635px; height: 350px"/>
      </div>
      <noscript>
       <a href="http://img-2.onedio.com/img/2r0/542c1b723f79027e36f0626a.jpg" target="_blank">
        <img src="http://img-2.onedio.com/img/bound/2r0/542c1b723f79027e36f0626a.jpg"/>
       </a>
      </noscript>
      <figcaption>
       <blockquote>
        <p>
         simsiz anlatc (Norton) uykusuzluktan muzdarip bir otomobil irketinde alan birisidir. Doktor ona daha fazla ila vermeyi reddeder ve kendisine yardmc olabilecek bir destek grubunu ziyaret etmesini nerir. Anlatc testis kanseri madurlar iin olan bir destek grubuna katlr ve orada Marla ile tanr; o da anlatc gen adam gibi hasta olmamasna ramen gruba katlmaktadr.Bir i gezisinden sonra evine dndnde bir patlama nedeniyle evinin tahrip olduunu grr ve yolculuk esnasnda tant, sabun satcs Tyler Durden' (
         <a href="/etiket/brad-pitt/5053aefb0228f60917601ab3" title="Brad Pitt">
          Brad Pitt
         </a>
         ) arayarak onunla bir barda buluur.
         <br/>
         <strong>
          Gizem, Dram
         </strong>
         <br/>
         <a class="external-link" data-trackimg="https://t.oned.io/onedio-inline-link.img" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0137523/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0137523/
         </a>
        </p>
       </blockquote>
      </figcaption>
     </figure>
    </section>

     <h2>
      1.Esaretin Bedeli /  The Shawshank Redemption (1994) | IMDb: 9.3
     </h2>
     <div class="hover-menu">
      <a class="facebook" data-fbui='{"method":"feed","display":"popup","link":"http://onedio.com/haber/surpriz-finaliyle-adeta-tokat-yemis-etkisi-yaratan-42-sok-edici-film-377944?entry=542d4083c18d1c317e812228","picture":"https://img-s2.onedio.com/id-542c1b99ef248e9a388caabb/rev-0/raw/s-5ae096e9612a97469769970dccd389dc855db775.jpg"}' href="#">
      </a>

      <a class="pinterest" href="https://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fonedio.com%2Fhaber%2Fsurpriz-finaliyle-adeta-tokat-yemis-etkisi-yaratan-42-sok-edici-film-377944%3Fentry%3D542d4083c18d1c317e812228&amp;description=S%C3%BCrpriz%20Finaliyle%20Adeta%20Tokat%20Yemi%C5%9F%20Etkisi%20Yaratan%2042%20%C5%9Eok%20Edici%20Film&amp;media=//img-s2.onedio.com/id-542c1b99ef248e9a388caabb/rev-0/raw/s-5ae096e9612a97469769970dccd389dc855db775.jpg" onclick="javascript:window.open(this.href, '', 'menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,height=600,width=600'); return false;">

      </a>
     </div>
     <figure>
      <div class="image wrapper">
       <img alt="Esaretin Bedeli /  The Shawshank Redemption (1994) | IMDb: 9.3" data-src="http://img-3.onedio.com/img/719/bound/2r0/542c1b99ef248e9a388caabb.jpg" src="/images/trans.png" style="margin-bottom: -32px; width: 635px; height: 350px"/>
      </div>

       <a href="http://img-3.onedio.com/img/2r0/542c1b99ef248e9a388caabb.jpg" target="_blank">
        <img src="http://img-3.onedio.com/img/bound/2r0/542c1b99ef248e9a388caabb.jpg"/>
       </a>
      </noscript>
      <figcaption>
       <blockquote>
        <p>
         Zeki bir bankac olan Andy Dufresne (Tim Robbins), kendisini aldatan karsn ve O'nun sevgilisini ldrd sulamasyla yarglanmaktadr. Tm itirazlarna ramen susuz olduuna mahkemeyi inandramaz ve mr boyu hapis cezasna arptrlr.Andy cezasn ekmek zere Shawsank Hapishanesi'ne gtrlr. Buras hayatnda grmedii kadar kt bir yerdir. Burada bir ok hakaret ve saldrya maruz kalacaktr. Andy tm bana gelenlere ramen hayata pozitif bakmay bilen bir adamdr. Bu bak asyla kendine bir ok dost edinir ve zamanla hapishanede sevilen biri olur.
         <br/>
         <strong>
          Su,Dram
         </strong>
         <br/>
         <a class="external-link" data-trackimg="https://t.oned.io/onedio-inline-link.img" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0111161/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0111161/
         </a>
        </p>
